    set community TTNet additive
    done
  endif
  set community TTNet additive
  set community TTNET_ANKARA additive
  set local-preference 135
  pass
end-policy

  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/24
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  #Accept-Route-cloudflare 
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^13335_') then
    set local-preference 200
    set community BGP-Customers
    set community tier1_global_community additive
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy Default-Route-IPv6-BGP-Export
  if destination in ipv6_def then
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy Default_and_BGP_Customer_Full
  if destination in (0.0.0.0/0) then
    done
  endif
  #Reject-Smaller-Than-/24#
  if destination in (0.0.0.0/0 ge 25) then
    drop
  endif
  #remove_rfc1918#
  if destination in (10.0.0.0/8 ge 32, 172.16.0.0/12 ge 32, 192.168.0.0/16 ge 32) then
    drop
  endif
  #Reject-Term#
  if community matches-any Dont-Announce-to-Customers then
    drop
  endif
  #International-Pops#
  if community matches-any International-Pops then
    drop
  endif
  #IP SLA
  if destination in (31.145.48.0/24) then
    done
  endif
  #Network-Statements#
  if community matches-any Bgp-Main-Network-Statements then
    done
  endif
  #Datacenter-Networks#
  if community matches-any Dc-Blocks then
    done
  endif
  #Announce-Upstreams#
  if as-path in Upstreams then
    done
  endif
  #Announce-Bgp-Customers#
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    done
  endif
  #Announce-Peerings#
  if community matches-any Peerings then
    done
  endif
  #Tr-1#
  if community matches-any TIER1-GLOBAL-COMMUNITY then
    done
  endif
  #Voice-Networks#
  if destination in (212.15.6.0/24, 212.15.13.0/24) then
    delete community all
    done
  endif
  #bt_nw#
  if destination in (213.194.65.0/24, 213.194.64.0/20) then
    done
  endif
  #geri_kalan#
  drop
end-policy

!
route-policy DRC_Mobil_IzmirINT-2_BGP_EXPORT
  #ONLY_ANNOUNCE_FROM_HERE
  if community matches-any DROP_COMM_ONLY_VCNO_ESENTEPE_INT2_PRI then
    drop
  endif
  #VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY
  if community matches-any VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY then
    drop
  endif
  #F5 CLOUD Service
  if community matches-any F5_CLOUD_DDOS_Servis_Anons_Kes or community matches-any F5_CLOUD_DDOS_ALWAYS_ON then
    drop
  endif
  #Only Announce TC Peering
  if community matches-any TC-Only then
    drop
  endif
  #BLACKHOLE
  if community matches-any VFNET-ARBOR-BLACKHOLE then
    set community VCNO-BLACKHOLE additive
    set community SEABONE-BLACKHOLE additive
    set community INTEROUTE-BLACKHOLE additive
    set community TT-BLACKHOLE additive
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any VCNO-BLACKHOLE then
    done
  endif
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT RFC1918
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT SEABONE IP TRANSIT PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^6762_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT TT PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^9121_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT INTEROUTE PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^8928_') then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT VCNO PEERING PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^3209_') then
    drop
  endif
  #MAGTICOM ANNOUNCE
  if community matches-any Magticom then
    done
  endif
  #TNAP REJECT
  if community matches-any TIER1-GLOBAL-COMMUNITY then
    drop
  endif
  #NETONE REJECT
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^12735_') then
    drop
  endif
  #DO NOT ANNOUNCE TO INTEROUTE
  if community matches-any DONT-ANNOUNCE-TO-INTEROUTE then
    drop
  endif
  #VODAFONE_MOBILE_Izmir2_Primary
  if community matches-any VF-GZM-GGSN or community matches-any VF-PSK-GGSN or community matches-any VF-ANT-GGSN or community matches-any VF-DYB-GGSN then
    prepend as-path 15924 5
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any VF-GZM-Catch_All or community matches-any VF-PSK-Catch_All then
    prepend as-path 15924 5
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any VF-TZL-GGSN or community matches-any VF-ESY-GGSN or community matches-any VF-ADN-GGSN or community matches-any VF-SAM-GGSN then
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any VF-TZL-Catch_All or community matches-any VF-ESY-Catch_All or community matches-any VF-ADN-Catch_All then
    done
  endif
  #Mobile_Other_Prefixes
  if community matches-any ANK_BOLGE_BGP_CUSTOMERS or community matches-any MOBILE_TUZLA then
    done
  endif
  if destination in NAT44_VF_BLOCKS_192 then
    done
  endif
  #INCITY_ISGs
  if community matches-any VFNET-ACIBADEM or community matches-any VFNET-GTEPE or community matches-any VFNET-FATIH or community matches-any VFNET-ATAKOY then
    prepend as-path 15924 5
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any VFNET-ATAKOY-2 or community matches-any VFNET-CAMLICA-ISG or community matches-any VFNET-ESENTEPE_FTTH then
    done
  endif

route-policy IBGP-EXPORT-TO-INTERNET-ROUTERS
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Voice-Customers then
    set community Customer-Voice-Subnetted additive
  endif
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    set next-hop self
    done
  endif
  if as-path is-local then
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

route-policy Izmir-VCNO-200G-IPv6-BGP-Import
  delete community all
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/48
  if destination in Smaller_than_48 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_Unique_Local_Addresses
  if destination in Reject-RFC4193-IPv6 then
    drop
  endif
  #Default
  if destination in ipv6_def then
    set local-preference 130
    set community VCNO_IPV6 additive
    done
  endif
  set local-preference 110
  set community VCNO_IPV6 additive
end-policy

route-policy VCNO-BGP-IZMIR-INT2-PRIMARY-EXPORT-PARENT
  if community matches-any IZMIR_DRC then
    apply DRC_Mobil_IzmirINT-2_BGP_EXPORT
    done
  elseif community matches-any VCNO_IZMIR_INT2_COMMUNITY_SECONDARY then
    prepend as-path 15924 4
    apply VCNO-BGP-IZMIR-INT2-PRIMARY-EXPORT
    done
  elseif community matches-any OTHER_THAN_VCNO_PRIMARY_IZMIR_INT2_COMMUNITY then
    prepend as-path 15924 7
    apply VCNO-BGP-IZMIR-INT2-PRIMARY-EXPORT
    done
  else
    apply VCNO-BGP-IZMIR-INT2-PRIMARY-EXPORT
  endif
  drop
end-policy

route-policy Default_and_IPT_Peering_Announce_without_VFTR
  if destination in (0.0.0.0/0) then
    done
  endif
  #Reject-Smaller-Than-/24#
  if destination in (0.0.0.0/0 ge 25) then
    drop
  endif
  #remove_rfc1918#
  if destination in (10.0.0.0/8 ge 32, 172.16.0.0/12 ge 32, 192.168.0.0/16 ge 32) then
    drop
  endif
  #Reject-Term#
  if community matches-any Dont-Announce-to-Customers then
    drop
  endif
  #International-Pops#
  if community matches-any International-Pops then
    drop
  endif
  #Datacenter-Networks#
  if community matches-any Dc-Blocks then
    drop
  endif
  #Announce-Bgp-Customers#
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    drop
  endif
  #Network-Statements#
  if community matches-any Bgp-Main-Network-Statements then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any VCNO_TUZLA then
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any VCNO_ESENTEPE then
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any SEABONE then
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any INTEROUTE then
    done
  endif
  #Announce-Upstreams#
  if as-path in Upstreams then
    done
  endif
  #Announce-Peerings#
  if community matches-any Peerings then
    done
  endif
  #Tr-1#
  if community matches-any TIER1-GLOBAL-COMMUNITY then
    done
  endif
  #geri_kalan#
  drop
end-policy
